```python
bin = np.linspace(500, 50000, 100)


pyplot.hist(x=df["No_of_Words"], bins=None, alpha=0.5, label='No of Words [Bin = none]')
pyplot.hist(x=df["No_of_Words"], bins=bin, alpha=0.5, label='No of Words [Bin = (500, 50000, 100)|]')
pyplot.xlim([0, 15000])
pyplot.title('Degree of No. of Words')
pyplot.xlabel('Words')
pyplot.ylabel('No. of Articles')
pyplot.legend(loc='upper right')
pyplot.show()



# ax = df.plot.hist(y="Log_of_words")
# pyplot.title('Range of Log(No. of Words) vs Frequency of Articles')
# pyplot.xlabel('Log(No. of Words)')
# pyplot.ylabel('No. of Articles')
# pyplot.savefig('Range of Log of No of Words vs Frequency of Articles.png')


bin = np.linspace(1, 2000, 2500)


pyplot.hist(x=df["Log_of_words"], bins=None, alpha=0.5, label='Log of Words [Bin = none]')
pyplot.hist(x=df["Log_of_words"], bins=bin, alpha=0.5, label='Log of Words [Bin = (1, 2000, 2500)]')
pyplot.xlim([5, 21])
pyplot.title('Degree of Log(No. of Words)')
pyplot.xlabel('Log(No. of Words)')
pyplot.ylabel('No. of Articles')
pyplot.legend(loc='upper right')
pyplot.show()


# ax = df.plot.hist(y="No_of_LNE", bins=np.arange(min(df["No_of_LNE"]), max(df["No_of_LNE"]) + 2, 2))
# pyplot.title('No. of LNEs vs Frequency of Articles')
# pyplot.xlabel('LNEs (NORP, FAC, ORG, LOC, EVENT)')
# pyplot.ylabel('No. of Articles')
# pyplot.xlim([0, 40])
# pyplot.savefig('No of LNEs vs Frequency of Articles.png')


bin = np.linspace(-1, 100, 100)


pyplot.hist(x=df["No_of_LNE"], bins=np.arange(min(df["No_of_LNE"]), max(df["No_of_LNE"]) + 2, 2), alpha=0.5, label='No of LNE [Bin = (min(df), max(df))]')
pyplot.hist(x=df["No_of_LNE"], bins=bin, alpha=0.5, label='No of LNE [Bin = (-1, 100, 100)]')
pyplot.xlim([0, 40])
pyplot.title('No. of LNEs vs Frequency of Articles')
pyplot.xlabel('LNEs (NORP, FAC, ORG, LOC, EVENT)')
pyplot.ylabel('No. of Articles')
pyplot.legend(loc='upper right')
pyplot.show()



# ax = df.plot.hist(y="Most_Frequent_LNE",  bins=np.arange(min(df["Most_Frequent_LNE"]), max(df["Most_Frequent_LNE"]) + 2, 2))
# pyplot.title('Count of Most Frequent LNE vs Frequency of Articles')
# pyplot.xlabel('Most Frequent LNE')
# pyplot.ylabel('No. of Articles')
# pyplot.xlim([0, 25])
# pyplot.savefig('Count of Most Frequent LNE vs Frequency of Articles.png')

bin = np.linspace(-1, 100, 100)

pyplot.hist(x=df["Most_Frequent_LNE"], bins=np.arange(min(df["Most_Frequent_LNE"]), max(df["Most_Frequent_LNE"]) + 2, 2), alpha=0.5, label='Most Frequent LNE [Bin = (min(df), max(df))]')
pyplot.hist(x=df["Most_Frequent_LNE"], bins=bin, alpha=0.5, label='Most Frequent LNE [Bin = (-1, 100, 100)]')
pyplot.xlim([0, 30])
pyplot.title('Degree of Most Frequent LNE')
pyplot.xlabel('Most Frequent LNE')
pyplot.ylabel('No. of Articles')
pyplot.legend(loc='upper right')
pyplot.show()


# ax = df.plot.hist(y="LNE_Density",  bins=np.arange(min(df["LNE_Density"]), max(df["LNE_Density"]) + 0.2, 0.2))
# pyplot.title('LNE Density vs Frequency of Articles')
# pyplot.xlabel('LNE Density(No_of_LNE/Log_of_words)')
# pyplot.ylabel('No. of Articles')
# pyplot.xlim([0, 4])
# pyplot.savefig('LNE Density vs Frequency of Articles3.png', dpi='figure', metadata=None,
#         bbox_inches=None, pad_inches=0.1,
#         facecolor='auto', edgecolor='auto',
#         backend=None)

bin = np.linspace(-1, 100, 1000)

pyplot.hist(x=df["LNE_Density"], bins=np.arange(min(df["LNE_Density"]), max(df["LNE_Density"]) + 0.2, 0.2), alpha=0.5, label='LNE Density [Bin = (min(df), max(df))]')
pyplot.hist(x=df["LNE_Density"], bins=bin, alpha=0.5, label='LNE Density [Bin = (-1, 100, 1000)]')
pyplot.xlim([0, 4])
pyplot.title('Degree of LNE Density')
pyplot.xlabel('LNE Density(No_of_LNE/Log_of_words)')
pyplot.ylabel('No. of Articles')
pyplot.legend(loc='upper right')
pyplot.show()
```

```python
bin = np.linspace(-10, 1000, 250)


pyplot.hist(x=list, bins=None, alpha=0.5, label='Log of Words [Bin = none]')
pyplot.hist(x=list, bins=bin, alpha=0.5, label='Log of Words [Bin = (-10, 1000, 250)]')
pyplot.xlim([5, 21])
pyplot.title('Degree of Log(No. of Words)')
pyplot.xlabel('Log(No. of Words)')
pyplot.ylabel('No. of Articles')
pyplot.legend(loc='upper right')
pyplot.show()
```
